<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 3; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(3);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<script>

    $("#divDashboardPaycheckDataView").data("AptaDataView")
        .SetFilterColumns('')
        .SetAutoLoad(true)
        .SetEditable(false)

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardPaycheckDataView', GridHeight: '160', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__DashboardPaycheckDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '160', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardPaycheckDataView', GridHeight: '160', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__DashboardPaycheckDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__DashboardPaycheckDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardPaycheckDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__DashboardPaycheckDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__DashboardPaycheckDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__DashboardPaycheckDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#SearchSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView();
        $('#tbFilterName__DashboardPaycheckDataView').val("");
        $("#searchSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__DashboardPaycheckDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'DashboardPaycheckDataView', GridHeight: '160', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardPaycheckDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#DashboardPaycheckDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divDashboardPaycheckDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___DashboardPaycheckDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'DashboardPaycheckDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardPaycheckDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "DashboardPaycheckDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("DashboardPaycheckDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ExportToExcel__DashboardPaycheckDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView();
        $("#divDashboardPaycheckDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("XLS");
    });

    $('#ExportToPdf__DashboardPaycheckDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView();
        $("#divDashboardPaycheckDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("PDF");
    });

    $('#ClearSearchSettings__DashboardPaycheckDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPaycheckDataView()
        $("#divDashboardPaycheckDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearFilterData();
        $('#divOptions__DashboardPaycheckDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__DashboardPaycheckDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__DashboardPaycheckDataView').css("padding-left", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__DashboardPaycheckDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__DashboardPaycheckDataView').css("margin-right", "3px");

        if ($("#dvGridSettings__DashboardLeaveRequestDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,

                $('#dvGridSettings__DashboardLeaveRequestDataView').html(result);
            },

                alert("Settings__DashboardLeaveRequestDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

<script>

    $("#divDashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("AptaDataView")
        .SetFilterColumns('')
        .SetAutoLoad(true)
        .SetEditable(false)

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardMyJobQueueDataView', GridHeight: '160', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '160', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardMyJobQueueDataView', GridHeight: '160', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardMyJobQueueDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#SearchSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView();
        $('#tbFilterName__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').val("");
        $("#searchSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'DashboardMyJobQueueDataView', GridHeight: '160', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#DashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divDashboardMyJobQueueDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___DashboardMyJobQueueDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'DashboardMyJobQueueDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "DashboardMyJobQueueDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("DashboardMyJobQueueDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ExportToExcel__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView();
        $("#divDashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("XLS");
    });

    $('#ExportToPdf__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView();
        $("#divDashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("PDF");
    });

    $('#ClearSearchSettings__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView()
        $("#divDashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearFilterData();
        $('#divOptions__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').css("padding-left", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').css("margin-right", "3px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___DashboardMyJobQueueDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("DashboardMyJobQueueDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView() {
        var gridName = 'DashboardMyJobQueueDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___DashboardMyJobQueueDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardMyJobQueueDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "DashboardMyJobQueueDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_DashboardMyJobQueueDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__DashboardMyJobQueueDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divDashboardMyJobQueueDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardPRApprovalsDataView', GridHeight: '160', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '160', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView() {

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'DashboardPRApprovalsDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

        LoadSettingsOnDemand__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'DashboardPRApprovalsDataView', GridHeight: '160', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#DashboardPRApprovalsDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divDashboardPRApprovalsDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___DashboardPRApprovalsDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'DashboardPRApprovalsDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "DashboardPRApprovalsDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("DashboardPRApprovalsDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___DashboardPRApprovalsDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("DashboardPRApprovalsDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView() {
        var gridName = 'DashboardPRApprovalsDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___DashboardPRApprovalsDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_DashboardPRApprovalsDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "DashboardPRApprovalsDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_DashboardPRApprovalsDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__DashboardPRApprovalsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divDashboardPRApprovalsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

	function EditPurchaseRequisitionPopup(id)
	{
		 var data, options;
		 var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divDashboardPRApprovalsDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        data = { Id: id, origin: 3, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: 3 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/EditMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
	   .SetContent(options)
	   .SetonClose(function () { $("#divDashboardPRApprovalsDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();})
       .SetTitle('Edit Purchase Requisition')
       .SetWidth(900)
       .SetHeight("90%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
	}

    $('#btnConfigure__Index').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        showConfigurePopup();
    });

    function showConfigurePopup() {

		var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowConfigure")
        .SetContent({ url: "/Home/ConfigureHomeScreen?enableGrids=" + 'True' + '~' + 'True' + '~' + 'False' + '~' + 'True' + '~' + 'True' + '~' + 'True'+ '~' + 'True'})
        .SetWidth('40%')
        .SetHeight('40%')
        .SetIsModal(true)
        .SetTitle('Configure')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    }

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/Home/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }
</script></body><canvas id="fxdriver-screenshot-canvas" style="display: none;" width="1251" height="1000"></canvas></html>
